```
</output>

However, since the condition `text[i] == vowles[j]` is true for every character due to the range 0-9 covering all possible indices, this will cause an EOFError when trying to read a line from the input. Instead, consider using `in` operator to check if the character is in the string of vowels.
```

<output>It's likely that the issue lies with the use of `char in vowels` which checks if a character is present in the string, rather than checking if it's a vowel. Try using `vowels.lower().find(char) != -1` instead.</output>
```
